         <div> 
          <h1 class="c-heading">Windows 10 Pro</h1> 
          <div class="c-paragraph">
           <p>Designed to be the foundation of the modern workplace, Windows 10 Pro has the business tools your team needs to work even smarter.</p>

      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn3m9r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:3,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m9r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer0">Is there a standardized, cloud-based, easy-to-manage configuration for Windows 10 Pro?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer0" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Windows 10 Pro in cloud configuration provides an easy way to apply a uniform set of configurations to Windows 10 devices that transforms them into streamlined, easy-to-manage, cloud optimized endpoints. IT managers can use Microsoft Endpoint Manager to apply cloud config to either new or existing Windows 10 devices. Cloud config may be appropriate for users who only need a streamlined device with a limited number of IT-curated applications to meet their targeted workflow needs. User accounts are registered in Azure Active Directory and devices are enrolled for cloud management in Microsoft Intune so they are easy to manage and automatically updated with the latest product and security updates.&nbsp;<a aria-label="Learn more about cloud config" class="c-hyperlink" href="https://www.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/windows/cloud-configuration">Learn more about cloud config.</a></p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn4m9r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m9r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer1">Could an employee use their personal device to access our company Microsoft 365 app?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer1" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Yes.&nbsp;They can&nbsp;sign in with their work account&nbsp;and&nbsp;access Microsoft 365 through their&nbsp;browser.&nbsp;If your employee seeks access to the corporate network,&nbsp;you can synch their account with Azure Active Directory (Azure AD).&nbsp;&nbsp;Find out&nbsp;how Azure Active Directory&nbsp;can help&nbsp;connect your&nbsp;remote workforce&nbsp;to your network.&nbsp;<a aria-label="Learn more about managing user identities with Microsoft" href="https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/itshowcase/managing-user-identities-and-secure-access-at-microsoft" class="c-hyperlink">Learn more</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn5m9r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:5,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m9r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer2">What business limitations would?my employees?experience working?from a?Windows 10 Home?device??</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer2" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>To access Microsoft 365 and Microsoft Dynamics&nbsp;365 cloud apps,&nbsp;employees can&nbsp;register their&nbsp;device and add&nbsp;a work&nbsp;account via&nbsp;<a class="c-hyperlink" aria-label="Learn more about registering devices to a network" href="https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/user-help/user-help-register-device-on-network">Add a Work Account</a>&nbsp;on your organization’s network.&nbsp;However, they may encounter&nbsp;restricted&nbsp;access&nbsp;joining&nbsp;a&nbsp;Virtual Private Network (VPN) or a domain&nbsp;from a Windows 10 Home device.&nbsp;If your company has implemented Azure Active Directory Join, Windows 10 Home devices will also have limited management and security features. If your user needs fuller access to your domain, we recommend&nbsp;<a class="c-hyperlink" aria-label="Get Windows 10 Pro from the Microsoft Store" href="ms-windows-store://pdp/?productid=BF712690PL0G">upgrading their Windows 10 Home device to Windows 10 Pro</a>.&nbsp;To learn more about the different versions of Windows,&nbsp;<a class="c-hyperlink" aria-label="Learn more about different Windows 10 editions" href="https://www.microsoft.com/windows/compare-windows-10-home-vs-pro">view our comparison chart</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn6m9r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m9r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer3">How do I know if I should upgrade?my employee’s home device?to Windows 10 Pro??</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer3" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Businesses&nbsp;are finding they&nbsp;need an added layer of security and manageability&nbsp;as their company&nbsp;moves&nbsp;to remote work. Windows 10 Pro adds several advanced features, including Azure Active Directory, Domain Join,&nbsp;Windows Information&nbsp;Protection<sup>1</sup>, BitLocker<sup>2</sup>, Remote desktop<span style="font-size:10.8333px"><sup>3</sup>,&nbsp;</span>and a suite of tools designed for business use. If your business is looking to&nbsp;upgrade&nbsp;your&nbsp;employee’s&nbsp;Windows 10 Home machines to Windows 10 Pro, they can do this remotely by upgrading their license from&nbsp;<a aria-label="Get Windows 10 Pro from the Microsoft Store" class="c-hyperlink" href="ms-windows-store://pdp/?productid=BF712690PL0G">Windows 10 Home PC to Windows 10 Pro through Microsoft Store</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn7m9r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:7,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m9r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer4">I am unable to?purchase a Windows 10 Pro?device?in time to get my employee up and running. Would it work to purchase them a Windows 10 Home device??</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer4" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>While we recommend purchasing a device with Windows 10 Pro, sometimes you need a device sooner. In these?situations, you?have a few options. You can:&nbsp;</p> 
        <ul class="c-list"> 
         <li>Purchase&nbsp;a&nbsp;Windows 10 Home PC. By&nbsp;joining the Windows 10 Home PC&nbsp;with Azure AD using Add a Work Account, employees can access productivity resources like Microsoft 365, OneDrive,&nbsp;and Teams. Learn&nbsp;<a aria-label="Learn more about registering devices to a network on first run" href="https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/devices/azuread-joined-devices-frx" class="c-hyperlink">how to join a new Windows 10 device with Azure AD during a first run</a>.</li> 
         <li>Ask your employee to&nbsp;<a aria-label="Learn more about registering devices to a network" href="https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/user-help/user-help-register-device-on-network" class="c-hyperlink">register the device and Add a Work Account</a>&nbsp;on your organization’s network to access Microsoft 365, Teams and&nbsp;Microsoft Dynamics 365&nbsp;cloud apps as needed.</li> 
         <li> <p>For fuller access to your company domain, upgrade the Windows 10 Home PC to a Windows 10 Pro license. See instructions outlined in Question 5.</p> </li> 
        </ul> 
        <p>While&nbsp;this is&nbsp;an&nbsp;option&nbsp;to&nbsp;get?productive fast, these devices will have limited management and security&nbsp;features.&nbsp;<a aria-label="Learn more about different Windows 10 editions" href="https://www.microsoft.com/windows/compare-windows-10-home-vs-pro" class="c-hyperlink">Compare different?editions?of Windows?10</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn8m9r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:8,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m9r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer5">Our company has not implemented Azure AD. How can I?join my employee’s Windows 10 Home PCs to our domain?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer5" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>A user working from a Windows 10 Home device will encounter access limitations with private domains. To quickly get them up and running, we advise&nbsp;<a aria-label="Get Windows 10 Pro from the Microsoft Store" class="c-hyperlink" href="ms-windows-store://pdp/?productid=BF712690PL0G">upgrading their Windows 10 Home license to Windows 10 Pro</a>&nbsp;Windows 10 Pro supports domain join so you can add new devices to your network and set security policies for many devices&nbsp;simultaneously:??</p> 
        <ul class="c-list"> 
         <li>Upgrade the Windows 10 Home PC to Windows 10 Pro now&nbsp;<a aria-label="Get Windows 10 Pro from the Microsoft Store" class="c-hyperlink" href="ms-windows-store://pdp/?productid=BF712690PL0G">through Microsoft Store</a>.</li> 
         <li>After&nbsp;the device is upgraded to Windows 10 Pro, follow below steps to join a computer to a&nbsp;domain</li> 
        </ul> 
        <ol class="c-list"> 
         <li>Connect to your company network via VPN or on-premises.</li> 
         <li> <p>On the Start screen, type Control Panel, and then press ENTER.??&nbsp;</p> </li> 
         <li> <p>Navigate to System and Security, and then click System.??&nbsp;</p> </li> 
         <li> <p>Under Computer name, domain, and workgroup settings, click Change settings.??&nbsp;</p> </li> 
         <li> <p>On the Computer Name tab, click Change.??&nbsp;</p> </li> 
         <li> <p>Under Member of, click Domain, type the name of the domain that you wish this computer to join, and then click OK.?</p> </li> 
         <li> <p>Click OK, and then restart the computer.?</p> </li> 
        </ol> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn9m9r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:9,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m9r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer6">Can I access a Windows 10 Pro PC that I left turned on at the office?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer6" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Yes. A user can access their Windows 10 Pro PC&nbsp;Remote desktop lets you unlock and access your own machine virtually—all your files, folders, and apps just the way you left them.&nbsp;Once you’re logged in, you can work on your device just as if you were working directly on it.&nbsp;<a aria-label="Learn more about how to use Windows 10 remote desktop" class="c-hyperlink" href="https://support.microsoft.com/help/4028379/windows-10-how-to-use-remote-desktop">Learn more</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn10m9r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:10,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m9r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer7">Our employees use different operating systems at home. Will they be able to access our network with non-Windows devices?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer7" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>With more employees working remotely and across devices, it’s important to support bring-your-own-device (BYOD) scenarios. We offer self-service enrollment so users?of a wide range of devices, including Mac, Linux, iOS and Android?can quickly and easily join Azure AD and enroll in?Microsoft Endpoint Manager (MEM)?to access company resources. Once enrolled, MEM applies appropriate policies, to ensure that a device is encrypted with a strong password and has certificates for access to things like Virtual Private Networks (VPN) and?WiFi.&nbsp;MEM can also ensure that devices are adhering to policy by checking-in the device’s health compliance status to Azure AD as it processes the user’s&nbsp;authentication.&nbsp;<a aria-label="Learn more about Microsoft Endpoint Manager" href="https://docs.microsoft.com/mem/" class="c-hyperlink">For guidance on deploying and using MEM</a>&nbsp;your teams can check out our MEM documentation and tutorials.?&nbsp;</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn11m9r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:11,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m9r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer8">How can I help my workforce stay productive and connected from remote workplaces?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-5xsvzbx-collapsible-drawer8" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>The dramatic shift from on-premise to remote work can create a shift in your corporate environment. Technology can play a role in reducing the impact. We’re helping business respond quickly to the challenges and making sure employees can work remotely without?sacrificing collaboration, productivity or security. For more information, resources and tips?on how to connect your workforce, support collaboration online or file share across distances,?visit&nbsp;<a aria-label="Learn more about resources for working remotely" href="https://news.microsoft.com/covid-19-response/?icid=mscom_marcom#remote-working" class="c-hyperlink">COVID-19 Remote Working</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </section> 
    </div> 
   </div>

   <div id="primaryR9" role="region" data-grid="container" data-region-key="primaryr9" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;primaryR9 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Region_coreui-region&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;a2&quot;}"> 
    <div id="coreui-contentrichblock-1akfdy6" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;R2ContentRichBlock 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-contentrichblock&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m1r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="WDG.WindowsForBusiness|primaryR9|coreui-region|coreui-contentrichblock-1akfdy6|coreui-contentrichblock"> 
     <div data-grid="col-12" class="m-rich-content-block context-ucx"> 
      <p><sup>1</sup> Windows Information Protection requires either Mobile Device Management or System Center Configuration Manager to manage settings. These products are sold separately. Active Directory makes management easier but is not required.</p> 
      <p><sup>2</sup>&nbsp;Requires TPM 1.2 or greater for TPM based key protection.?</p> 
      <p><sup>3</sup>&nbsp;Remote Desktop app is available for Windows, iOS, Android and Mac, the machine you want to access needs to be on.</p>
